The Power of Attorney shall remain in full force and  effect until the undersigned is no longer required to file Forms 3, 4 and 5 with regard to his or her  ownership of or transactions in securities of the Company, unless earlier revoked in writing. Tracy  Lowe and Carli Penney are not assuming any of the undersigned&#8217;s responsibilities to comply with  Section 16 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended.
